T-independent: `c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*|epsilon|+1)+c9)`. sin(log(...)) ≠ epsilon^c.
Candidate 24 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 25:
`T*c0*epsilon + T^c1*c2*epsilon^(1/3) + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*|epsilon|+1)+c8)`

If c1=1: T-dependent = `T*(c0*epsilon + c2*epsilon^(1/3))`. Missing `T` term. Also epsilon^(1/3) ≠ epsilon^0.5976 (fixed exponent 1/3 vs free).

Wait, the exponent 1/3 is hardcoded. GT needs ~0.5976. 1/3 ≈ 0.333. These are different and the exponent is fixed, not a free constant.

Also missing `T` term and sin(log) ≠ power law.
Candidate 25 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 26:
`T*c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + T*c2*epsilon + T*c3 + T*c4*exp(c5*epsilon)*|epsilon|^c6 + c7*epsilon/(c8+epsilon^2)`

If c1=0 and c5=0: T-dependent = `T*(c0+c3+c2*epsilon+c4*|epsilon|^c6)` = `T*(const + c2*epsilon + c4*epsilon^c6)` ✓

T-independent: `c7*epsilon/(c8+epsilon^2)`. This is a rational function, not `A*epsilon + B + C*epsilon^D`. For large epsilon, this goes to c7/epsilon → 0, while GT's T-independent part grows. Cannot match.
Candidate 26 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 27:
`T*c0 + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon+c3) + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6 + c7*epsilon^c8`

If c2=0: T-dependent = `T*(c0 + c1*sin(c3))` = `T*const`. Missing `T*epsilon` and `T*epsilon^c`.
Candidate 27 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 28:
`T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*exp(T*c5)*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*epsilon/(c8+epsilon)`

Has `exp(T*c5)` — if c5=0, becomes constant. Then T-dependent = `T*(c0*epsilon+c1)`. Missing `T*epsilon^c`.
Candidate 28 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 29:
`T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8))`

Missing `T*epsilon^c`. exp(sin(...)) can't match power law.
Candidate 29 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 30:
`T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + T*c2*|epsilon|^c3 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*epsilon^5*sin(T*c7+c8) + c9*epsilon`

T-dependent: `T*(c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*|epsilon|^c3)` ✓ (with domain constraint, |epsilon|=epsilon)
Plus `c6*epsilon^5*sin(T*c7+c8)` — this has T inside sin, which is non-linear in T. If c7=0: `c6*epsilon^5*sin(c8)` = constant*epsilon^5. 

If c7=0: T-independent = `c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*epsilon^5*sin(c8) + c9*epsilon`
If c5=0: `c4 + c6*epsilon^5*sin(c8) + c9*epsilon`

We need T-independent = `A*epsilon + B + C*epsilon^0.5976`. We have `c4 + c9*epsilon + const*epsilon^5`. The epsilon^5 term can't match epsilon^0.5976 (5 is fixed). Set c6=0 to eliminate it. Then T-independent = `c4 + c9*epsilon`. Missing `epsilon^0.5976`.
Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 31:
`T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + T*c2*epsilon^c3 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*epsilon^5*sin(T*c7+c8) + c9*epsilon`

T-dependent: `T*(c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*epsilon^c3)` ✓
`c6*epsilon^5*sin(T*c7+c8)`: if c7=0, becomes `c6*epsilon^5*sin(c8)`.

If c5=0 and c7=0: T-independent = `c4 + c6*epsilon^5*sin(c8) + c9*epsilon`
Need `A*epsilon + B + C*epsilon^0.5976`. The epsilon^5 is fixed exponent. Set c6=0: `c4 + c9*epsilon`. Missing `epsilon^c3` in T-independent.

GT requires epsilon^0.5976 in BOTH T-dependent and T-independent parts. This candidate has epsilon^c3 only in T-dependent.
Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 32:
No T dependence at all (no T variable). GT depends on T.

### Candidate 33:

### Candidate 34:

T-dependent: `T*(c0 + c1*epsilon^c2)`. Missing `T*epsilon`.

Wait — if c2=1, then `T*(c0 + c1*epsilon)`. But then missing `T*epsilon^0.5976`.

We need three T-dependent basis functions: constant, epsilon, epsilon^c. This has only two: constant and epsilon^c2. If c2=1, we get constant and epsilon but lose epsilon^c. If c2=0.5976, we get constant and epsilon^0.5976 but lose epsilon.

T-independent: `c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*epsilon + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*epsilon+1)+c9)`. sin(log(...)) and exp can't match power law + linear + constant.
